  <span m='3711430'>you</span> <span m='3711610'>do</span> <span m='3712160'>a</span>
  <span m='3712260'>pulsed</span> <span m='3713010'>observation,</span> <span m='3713720'>which</span>
  <span m='3713910'>is</span> <span m='3714010'>a</span> <span m='3714110'>strong</span>

  <span m='4070930'>varying</span> <span m='4071490'>term,</span> <span m='4072450'>it</span>
